* Reusable functions

#+begin_src R :results silent :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
  generate_analysis <- function(day) {
    # Convert RST to CSV
    system(paste0("aky_converter --no-links ", day, "/rastro-*.rst | pj_dump | grep ^State > ", day, ".csv"))

    # Read
    df <- read_csv(paste0(day, ".csv"), col_names = FALSE, progress = FALSE, show_col_types = FALSE) |>
      select(rank = X2, start = X4, end = X5, duration = X6, state = X8) |>
      mutate(rank = as.integer(gsub("rank", "", rank))) |>
      mutate(state = as.factor(state))

    # Define true start and end
    s.start <- df |>
      filter(state == "MPI_Recv") |>
      filter(start == min(start)) |>
      pull(start)

    s.end <- df |>
      filter(state == "MPI_Waitall") |>
      filter(end == max(end)) |>
      pull(end)

    # Consider only the middle of the execution
    df.filtered <- df |>
      filter(!(state %in% c("MPI_Recv", "MPI_Send", "MPI_Cart_rank", "MPI_Wtime"))) |>
      filter(start >= s.start) |>
      filter(end <= s.end)

    # Consider only when everyone is working
    df.filtered |>
      group_by(rank) |>
      arrange(start) |>
      slice(1) |>
      ungroup() |>
      arrange(start) |>
      slice(n()) |>
      pull(start) -> s.start

    df.filtered2 <- bind_rows(
      df.filtered |>
        filter(start <= s.start & end >= s.start) |>
        mutate(start = s.start),
      df.filtered |>
        filter(!(start <= s.start & end >= s.start)) |>
        filter(start >= s.start)
    )

    # Stats
    df.filtered2 |>
      group_by(rank) |>
      summarize(
        MPI.time = sum(duration),
        Makespan.time = max(end) * length(unique(rank))
      ) |>
      mutate(P = round(MPI.time / Makespan.time * 100, 2)) |>
      write_csv(paste0(day, "_mpi_time_per_rank.csv"), progress = FALSE) |>
      ungroup() |>
      filter(rank != 0) |>
      summarize(
        MPI.time = sum(MPI.time),
        Makespan.time = sum(Makespan.time)
      ) |>
      mutate(P = round(MPI.time / Makespan.time * 100, 2)) |>
      write_csv(paste0(day, "_mpi_time_global.csv"))

    # Plot
    p <- df.filtered2 |>
      ggplot(aes(
        fill = state, color = state,
        xmin = start, xmax = end,
        ymin = rank - 0.3, ymax = rank + 0.3
      )) +
      geom_rect()
    ggsave(paste0(day, ".pdf"), p)
    print(p)
  }
#+end_src

* Advancements
** 2025-09-27

*Problem*: the hash of the output produced *in parallel* (sequentially works fine) by our application did not match that of the original.

*Partial solution*:
The study object was improperly using the wrong indices for the anisotropy variables: since every worker computes the precomputation and anisotropy
variables on their own (for the sake of having work to do before receiving the assigned portion of the cube from the coordinator), they were wrongly
using their local indices (worker indices) instead of the global ones, which are the ones used by the original application.

** 2025-09-29

*Problem*: the hash of the output produced *in parallel* (sequentially works fine) by our application did not match that of the original.
*Final solution*:
The original application utilizes cross derivatives between X and Y, which requires diagonals to be exchanged between halo regions.
This wasn't present in our implementation, so diagonal communications were implemented.

*Problem*: the source insertion was poorly handled, making the output hash differ from the proper one.
*Solution*: make every worker insert the source on their own on *pc* and *qc*, which ensures they have the correct data available to compute with.

** 2025-09-30

*Problem*: *MPI_cart_rank* was being called every iteration by every worker in order to find their neighbours, which is an unnecessary MPI overhead.
*Solution*: bringing all these calls to the beginning of the application

*Problem*: *MPI_Waitall* was being called twice per iteration with the purpose of waiting the two halo receivings (for *pp* and *qp*), introducing
an unnecessary MPI overhead.
*Solution*: merged both requests into one larger *MPI_Request* array before calling a single *MPI_Waitall*.
** 2025-10-16
Collected new results from execution. Factors:
- ~size_x~: 500
- ~size_y~: 500
- ~size_z~: 500
- ~absorption~: 3
- ~dx~: 0.03
- ~dy~: 0.03
- ~dz~: 0.03
- ~dt~: 0.000110
- ~tmax~: 30
Results:
#+begin_src R :results value :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
  generate_analysis(here::here("analysis/2025-10-16"))
#+end_src

** 2025-10-20
Modularized the project to allow for different backends. Two major changes were required:
1. Modifying the ~Makefile~ to allow for different environments
2. Modifying the interior computation and boundaries computation functions to use a function from
   a separate file, which source is provided by the Makefile based on the variables provided.
No major issues arised, the parallel and sequential version's hashes remain the same.
The only problem faced was that MPI automatically binds processes to cores, which makes multithreading
in a single machine (for testing purposes) impossible. Therefore, a flag was passed to ~mpicc~ to avoid
such binding.

** 2025-10-22
Found a potential bug in ~worker.c~. The ~MPI_Wait~ calls were being executed all at once
by the end of the loop, which could cause a buffer overflow. These wait calls have been brought to the
last lines of the main worker loop.

day <- "2025-10-16"

    # Convert RST to CSV
    system(paste0("aky_converter --no-links ", day, "/rastro-*.rst | pj_dump | grep ^State > ", day, ".csv"))

    # Read
    df <- read_csv(paste0(day, ".csv"), col_names = FALSE, progress = FALSE, show_col_types = FALSE) |>
      select(rank = X2, start = X4, end = X5, duration = X6, state = X8) |>
      mutate(rank = as.integer(gsub("rank", "", rank))) |>
      mutate(state = as.factor(state))

    # Define true start and end
    s.start <- df |>
      filter(state == "MPI_Recv") |>
      filter(start == min(start)) |>
      pull(start)

    s.end <- df |>
      filter(state == "MPI_Waitall") |>
      filter(end == max(end)) |>
      pull(end)

    # Consider only the middle of the execution
    df.filtered <- df |>
      filter(!(state %in% c("MPI_Recv", "MPI_Send", "MPI_Cart_rank", "MPI_Wtime"))) |>
      filter(start >= s.start) |>
      filter(end <= s.end)

    # Consider only when everyone is working
    df.filtered |>
      group_by(rank) |>
      arrange(start) |>
      slice(1) |>
      ungroup() |>
      arrange(start) |>
      slice(n()) |>
      pull(start) -> s.start

    df.filtered2 <- bind_rows(
      df.filtered |>
        filter(start <= s.start & end >= s.start) |>
        mutate(start = s.start),
      df.filtered |>
        filter(!(start <= s.start & end >= s.start)) |>
        filter(start >= s.start)
    )
print(s.start)
print(s.end)


    # Stats
    df.filtered2 |>
      group_by(rank) |>
      summarize(
        MPI.time = sum(duration),
        Makespan.time = max(end) * length(unique(rank))

*** New analysis
#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
df |>
  group_by(rank) |>
  arrange(start) |>
  filter(state == "MPI_Irecv") |>
  slice(1) |>
  select(rank, kickoff = start) -> df.start

df |>
  group_by(rank) |>
  arrange(start) |>
  filter(state == "MPI_Waitall") |>
  slice(n()) |>
  select(rank, kickend = end) -> df.end

df |>
  left_join(df.start, by = join_by(rank)) |>
  left_join(df.end, by = join_by(rank)) |>  
  filter(start >= kickoff) |>
  filter(end <= kickend) |>
  group_by(rank) |>
  arrange(start) |>
  mutate(mark = state == "MPI_Waitall") |>
  mutate(iteration = 1 + cumsum(mark)) |>
  mutate(iteration = case_when(state == "MPI_Waitall" ~ iteration - 1,
                               TRUE ~ iteration)) |>
  select(-mark) -> df.iteration

df.iteration |>
  filter(state == "MPI_Isend") |>
  ggplot(aes(x = duration)) +
  geom_density() + #histogram(bins=1000) +
  facet_wrap(~state)
#+end_src

#+RESULTS:

  select(rank, duration, state) |>

  filter(duration < 10) -> df.2

  filter((state %in% c("MPI_Waitall"))) |>
  filter(duration > 10) |>
  # brutal
  mutate(duration = mean.duration.waitall.faster) -> df.3

  group_by(rank) |>

*** Conclusions
- Imbalance communication (likely due to four nodes usage)
  - We should use a number of nodes that has a cubic root
*** Future work
- Support to CUDA in the current version as a new backend
- Ghost cell fine tuning methodology with simulation (simgrid)
- Executions in Grid5000 larger clusters
  - Lille chuc because of 4 x Nvidia A100 (40 GiB)
  - If doesnt work, fallback to CPU-only with larger clusters such as
    - Nancy gros
    - Grenoble dahu

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
options(crayon.enabled=FALSE)
suppressMessages(library(tidyverse))
#+end_src

#+RESULTS:

*** Function
#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
parse_mpip <- function(file_path) {
    path_parts <- str_match(file_path, "/([0-9]+)/([0-9]+)/dc\\.mpiP$")

    if (any(is.na(path_parts))) {
        warning(paste("Could not parse path structure for:", file_path))
        return(NULL)
    }

    run_number <- as.integer(path_parts[2])
    problem_size <- as.integer(path_parts[3])

    lines <- readLines(file_path, warn = FALSE)

    time_idx <- grep("@.*Time.*seconds", lines)

    if (length(time_idx) > 0) {
        subset_lines <- lines[time_idx:min(time_idx + 50, length(lines))]

        agg_line_idx <- grep("^\\s*\\*\\s+[0-9.]+\\s+[0-9.]+\\s+([0-9.]+)$", subset_lines)

        parsed_data <- NULL

        if (length(agg_line_idx) > 0) {
            agg_line <- subset_lines[agg_line_idx[1]]
            parsed_data <- str_match(agg_line, "^\\s*\\*\\s+([0-9.]+)\\s+([0-9.]+)\\s+([0-9.]+)$")
        } else {
            task0_line_idx <- grep("^\\s*0\\s+[0-9.]+\\s+[0-9.]+\\s+([0-9.]+)$",
                subset_lines)
            if (length(task0_line_idx) > 0) {
                agg_line <- subset_lines[task0_line_idx[1]]
                parsed_data <- str_match(agg_line, "^\\s*0\\s+([0-9.]+)\\s+([0-9.]+)\\s+([0-9.]+)$")
            }
        }

        if (!is.null(parsed_data) && !any(is.na(parsed_data))) {
            total_time <- as.numeric(parsed_data[2])
            mpi_time <- as.numeric(parsed_data[3])
            computation_time <- total_time - mpi_time

            return(data.frame(run = run_number, problem_size = problem_size, mpi_time = mpi_time,
                computation_time = computation_time, total_time = total_time))
        }
    }

    NULL
}
#+end_src

#+RESULTS:
*** Read
#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
parse_mpip("./analysis/2026-01-20/60/512/dc.mpiP")
#+end_src

#+RESULTS:
*** Function

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
options(crayon.enabled=FALSE)
suppressMessages(library(tidyverse))
lets_read_our_csv <- function (FILENAME) {
  read_csv(FILENAME,
           show_col_types=FALSE,
           progress=FALSE,
           col_names = c("Nature",
                         "Container",
                         "Type",
                         "Start", "End", "Duration",
                         "Imbrication", "Value")) |>
    select(-Type) |>
    select(-Imbrication) |>
    mutate(Container = as.integer(gsub("rank-?", "", Container))) |>
    mutate(Value = gsub("^PMPI_", "MPI_", Value)) |>
    mutate(Rank = Container) |>
    mutate(Operation = as.factor(Value)) |>
    filter(Operation != "MPI_Comm_size") |>
    filter(Operation != "MPI_Allgather") |>
    filter(Operation != "MPI_Finalize") |>
    filter(Operation != "MPI_Init") |>
    filter(Operation %in% c("MPI_Recv", "MPI_Irecv",
                            "MPI_Send", "MPI_Isend", "MPI_Waitall"))
}
#+end_src

#+RESULTS:

*** Read

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
options(crayon.enabled=FALSE)
suppressMessages(library(tidyverse))
tibble(FILE = c("2026-02-19/1/256/dc.csv", "../dc.csv")) |>
  mutate(DATA = map(FILE, lets_read_our_csv)) |>
  unnest(DATA) |>
  group_by(FILE, Operation) |>
  summarize(N = n(), Mean = mean(Duration), .groups="drop") |>
  arrange(Operation, FILE) |>
  mutate(Total = N * Mean) |>
  mutate(P = Total / sum(Total) * 100)
#+end_src

*** Compute MSamples/s

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
tibble(FILE = c("2026-02-19/1/256/dc.csv")) |>
  mutate(DATA = map(FILE, lets_read_our_csv)) |>
  unnest(DATA) |>
  filter(Operation != "MPI_Allgather") |>
  filter(Operation != "MPI_Finalize") |>
  filter(Operation != "MPI_Init") |>
  arrange(Start) -> df

# Get last MPI_Send
df |>
  filter(Rank == 0) |>
  filter(Operation == "MPI_Send") |>
  arrange(-End) |>
  pull(End) |>
  max() -> t.start

# Get first MPI_Recv
df |>
  filter(Rank == 0) |>
  filter(Operation == "MPI_Recv") |>
  arrange(-Start) |>
  pull(Start) |>
  min() -> t.end

walltime = (t.end-t.start)
walltime
  

df |>
  filter(Start >= t.start) |>
  filter(End <= t.end) |>
  ggplot(aes(xmin=Start,xmax=End, ymin=Rank, ymax=Rank+0.9, fill=Operation)) + geom_rect()
#+end_src

** 2026-04-03
:PROPERTIES:
:header-args: :tangle "do-2026-04-03.R" :tangle-mode (identity #o755) :shebang "#!/usr/bin/Rscript"
:END:
*** The aggregation framework (starvz-inspired)
**** integrateStepFunc
#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
source("integrateStepFunc.R")
#+end_src

#+RESULTS:

**** StarVZ functions copied "as is"
#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
integrate.stepfunc.Rcpp <- function(inter, b, f) integrateStepFunc(inter, c(-Inf, b, Inf), c(0, f, 0))

getBreaks <- function(dfv = NULL) {
  if (is.null(dfv)) {
    return(NULL)
  }
  breaks <- c(dfv$Start, dfv$End[length(dfv$End)])
  return(breaks)
}

getSlices <- function(dfv = NULL, step = 100) {
  tstart <- dfv %>%
    .$Start %>%
    min()
  tend <- (dfv %>% .$End %>% max())
  # TODO: Explain how we ignore the last slice if tend is not multiple
  # of step. This will make us ignore all behavior from the beginning
  # of that last slice until tend. This is unimportant for visualization
  # purposes but it can be important for stats. On that case, replace
  # the second argument by =tend+step= to make sure all data is considered.
  slices <- c(seq(0, tend, step), tend)
  return(slices)
}

remyTimeIntegration <- function(dfv = NULL, slices = NULL) {
  if (is.null(dfv)) {
    return(NULL)
  }
  if (is.null(slices)) {
    return(NULL)
  }

  # Define breaks
  breaks <- getBreaks(dfv)

  # Define values on breaks
  values <- dfv$Value

  result <- integrate.stepfunc.Rcpp(slices, breaks, values)

  return(result)
}

remyTimeIntegrationPrep <- function(dfv = NULL, myStep = 100) {
  if (is.null(dfv)) {
    return(NULL)
  }
  if (nrow(dfv) == 0) {
    return(NULL)
  }
  mySlices <- getSlices(dfv, step = myStep)
  tibble(Slice = mySlices, Value = c(remyTimeIntegration(dfv, slices = mySlices), 0) / myStep)
}
#+end_src

#+RESULTS:

**** NEW StarVZ adapted functions so they can be faster

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
do_the_aggregation <- function(df, step_width) {
  df |>
  select(ResourceId = Container, Task = Value, Start, End) |>
    arrange(ResourceId, Task, Start) |>
    group_by(ResourceId, Task) |>
    reframe(
      bind_rows(
        tibble(
          Start = Start,
          End   = End,
          Active = 1
        ),
        tibble(
          Start = End,
          End   = lead(Start),
          Active = 0
        ) |> filter(!is.na(End)),
        tibble(
          Start = 0,
          End   = first(Start),
          Active = 0
        )
      )
    ) |>
    rename(Value = Active) |>
    arrange(ResourceId, Task, Start) |>
    group_by(ResourceId, Task) |>
    do(remyTimeIntegrationPrep(., myStep = step_width)) |>
    mutate(Start = Slice,
           End = lead(Slice),
           Duration = End - Start) |>
    ungroup() |>
    na.omit() 
}
#+end_src

#+RESULTS:

**** The reference aggregation

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
do_the_reference_aggregation <- function(df, nb_intervals) {
  df |> pull(Start) |> min() -> t.start
  df |> pull(End) |> max() -> t.end
  step_width = (t.end-t.start)/nb_intervals
  df |>
    do_the_aggregation(step_width) |>
    # make it has the same columns for our do_the_viz fun
    mutate(Slice = round(Slice / step_width)) |>
    rename(Container = ResourceId,
           Value = Task,
           Percent = Value,
           StartTS = Start, # Start of the timeslice (TS)
           EndTS = End,     # End of the timeslice (TS)
           DurationTS = Duration) |> # Duration of the timeslice (TS)
    mutate(Time.Sum = Percent * DurationTS)
}
#+end_src

#+RESULTS:

**** Plot function (do-the-viz)

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
library(patchwork)
do_the_viz <- function(df, has.summary = FALSE)
{
  df |>
    rename(Rank = Container) -> df
  
  # Prep Y labels
  df |>
    distinct(Rank) |>
    arrange(Rank) |>
    mutate(Position = 0:(n()-1)) |>
    mutate(Label = Position) -> yconfm
  
  df |>
    filter(Time.Sum != 0) |>
    group_by(Rank, Slice, StartTS, EndTS, DurationTS, Value) |>
    summarize(Time.Sum = sum(Time.Sum), .groups="drop_last") |>
    ungroup(Value) |>
    arrange(Value) |>
    mutate(TaskHeight = Time.Sum / DurationTS) |>
    mutate(TaskPosition = cumsum(TaskHeight) - TaskHeight) |>
    left_join(yconfm, by="Rank") |>
    ggplot() +
    scale_y_continuous(
      breaks = yconfm$Position,
      labels = yconfm$Label
    ) +    
    geom_rect(alpha=.5, aes(
      fill = Value,
      xmin = StartTS,
      xmax = EndTS,
      ymin = Position + TaskPosition,
      ymax = Position + (TaskPosition + TaskHeight)
    )) +
    my_style() +
    theme(axis.title.x = element_blank(),
          axis.text.x = element_blank()) +
    ylab("Rank [index]") +
    xlab("Time [seconds]") -> p

# summary plot
  df |>
    filter(Time.Sum != 0) |>
    group_by(Slice, StartTS, EndTS, DurationTS, Value) |>
    summarize(N=n(), Time.Sum = sum(Time.Sum), .groups="drop_last") |>
    ungroup(Value) |>
    arrange(Value) |>
    mutate(TaskHeight = Time.Sum / (DurationTS * N)) |>
    mutate(TaskPosition = cumsum(TaskHeight) - TaskHeight) |>
    ggplot() +
    coord_cartesian(ylim=c(0,1)) +
    geom_rect(alpha=.5, aes(
      fill = Value,
      xmin = StartTS,
      xmax = EndTS,
      ymin = TaskPosition,
      ymax = (TaskPosition + TaskHeight)
    )) +
    my_style() +
    theme(legend.position="none") +
    ylab("Load [%]") +
    xlab("Time [seconds]") -> p.summary
 
  if (has.summary) {
    p / p.summary + plot_layout(heights = c(1, 0.15))
  }else{
    p
  }
}
#+end_src

#+RESULTS:

**** My style

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
my_style <- function() {
  list(
#    scale_fill_brewer(palette = "Set1"),
#    scale_color_brewer(palette = "Set1"),
    scale_fill_manual(
      values = c(
        MPI_Irecv  = "#4DAF4A",  # Set1 green
        MPI_Isend  = "#E41A1C",  # Set1 red
        MPI_Waitall = "#377EB8", # Set1 blue
        Compute     = "#FFD92F"  # yellow        
      )
    ),
    theme_bw(base_size = 16),
    theme(legend.position="top"),
    theme(
      legend.title = element_blank(),
      plot.margin = unit(c(0, 0, 0, 0), "cm"),
      legend.spacing = unit(1, "mm"),
      legend.justification = "left",
      legend.box.spacing = unit(0, "pt"),
      legend.box.margin = margin(0, 0, 0, 0),
      axis.text.x = element_text(angle=45, vjust=1, hjust=1)
    ))
}
#+end_src

#+RESULTS:

*** Functions
**** Read

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
our_read_function <- function(f) {
  read_csv(f,
           show_col_types=FALSE,
           progress=FALSE,
           col_names = c("Nature",
                         "Container",    
                         "Type",
                         "Start",
                         "End",
                         "Duration",
                         "Imbrication",
                         "Value")) |> # name of the Operation
    mutate(Container = as.integer(gsub("rank-?", "", Container))) |>
    mutate(Value = str_trim(gsub("^\\s*PMPI_", "MPI_", str_trim(Value)))) |>    
    mutate(Value = as.factor(Value)) |>
    filter(Value %in% c("MPI_Irecv", "MPI_Isend", "MPI_Waitall")) |>
    mutate(Value = factor(Value, levels=c("MPI_Irecv", "MPI_Isend", "MPI_Waitall"))) -> df
# Keep only the part that interest us
# Highly dependent on parallel design
  core_start <- df |>    
    filter(Value == "MPI_Irecv") |>    
    pull(Start) |>    
    min()    
  core_end <- df |>    
    filter(Value == "MPI_Waitall") |>    
    pull(End) |>    
    max()    
  df <- df |>    
    filter(Start < core_end) |>    
    filter(End > core_start) |>    
    mutate(Start = pmax(Start, core_start), End = pmin(End, core_end), Duration = End - Start)
# Return the data frame
  return(df)
}
#+end_src

#+RESULTS:
**** Compute

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
add_compute_state <- function(df) {

  compute <- df |>
    arrange(Container, Start) |>
    group_by(Container) |>
    mutate(next_start = lead(Start)) |>
    filter(!is.na(next_start), next_start > End) |>
    transmute(
      Nature = "State",
      Container,
      Type = "MPI_STATE",
      Start = End,
      End = next_start,
      Duration = End - Start,
      Imbrication = 0,
      Value = factor("Compute", levels = c(levels(df$Value), "Compute"))
    )

  bind_rows(df, compute) |>
    arrange(Container, Start) |>
    ungroup()
}
#+end_src

#+RESULTS:

**** Plot ST

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
our_st_plot <- function(data) {
  library(dplyr)
  library(ggplot2)

  data %>%
    rename(Rank = Container) |>
    mutate(
      ymin = Rank - 0.45,
      ymax = Rank + 0.45
    ) %>%
    ggplot() +
    geom_rect(
      aes(
        xmin = Start,
        xmax = End,
        ymin = ymin,
        ymax = ymax,
        fill = Value
      ),
      colour = NA
    ) +
    labs(
      x = "Time",
      y = "Rank",
      fill = "Value"
    ) +
    theme_bw(base_size = 12) +
    theme(
      panel.grid = element_blank(),
      strip.text = element_text(face = "bold"),
      legend.position = "bottom"
    ) +
    my_style()
}
#+end_src

#+RESULTS:
**** Summary per Task

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
summary_per_operation <- function(dfa) {
  dfa |>
    group_by(Value) |>
    summarise(
      n      = n(),
      mean   = mean(Duration, na.rm = TRUE),
      sd     = sd(Duration, na.rm = TRUE),
      min    = min(Duration, na.rm = TRUE),
      p25    = quantile(Duration, 0.25, na.rm = TRUE),
      median = median(Duration, na.rm = TRUE),
      p75    = quantile(Duration, 0.75, na.rm = TRUE),
      p90    = quantile(Duration, 0.90, na.rm = TRUE),
      p99    = quantile(Duration, 0.99, na.rm = TRUE),
      max    = max(Duration, na.rm = TRUE),
      .groups = "drop"
    )
}
#+end_src

#+RESULTS:
**** Plot the summary per task
#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
plot_summary_per_operation <- function(df) {

  ggplot(df, aes(x = Value)) +

    # min → max range
    geom_linerange(aes(ymin = min, ymax = max),
                   linewidth = 0.6, alpha = 0.5) +

    # interquartile range
    geom_linerange(aes(ymin = p25, ymax = p75),
                   linewidth = 3) +

    # median
    geom_point(aes(y = median), size = 3, shape = 21, fill = "white") +

    # p90 and p99 markers
    geom_point(aes(y = p90), shape = 17, size = 2) +
    geom_point(aes(y = p99), shape = 18, size = 2) +

    # sample size label
    geom_text(aes(y = max, label = paste0("n=", n)),
              vjust = -0.5, size = 3) +

#    scale_y_log10() +

    labs(
      x = "Operation",
      y = "Duration",
    ) +

    theme_bw()
}
#+end_src

#+RESULTS:
**** Plot total time per operation
#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
plot_total_time_per_operation <- function(df) {

  df |>
    group_by(Value) |>
    summarise(total_duration = sum(Duration, na.rm = TRUE),
              .groups = "drop") |>
    ggplot(aes(x = Value, y = total_duration, fill = Value)) +
    
    geom_col(width = 0.7) +
    
    geom_text(aes(label = scales::scientific(total_duration)),
              vjust = -0.3, size = 3) +
    
    labs(
      x = "Operation",
      y = "Total Duration",
    ) +
    
    theme_bw() +
    theme(legend.position = "none")
}
#+end_src

*** Do the thing

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
options(crayon.enabled=FALSE)
suppressMessages(library(tidyverse))
suppressMessages(library(fs))
suppressMessages(library(patchwork))
tibble(FILE = dir_ls("2026-04-03", pattern="*.csv")) |>
  mutate(KEY = str_remove(basename(FILE), "\\.csv$")) |>  
  mutate(DATA = map(FILE, our_read_function)) |>
  mutate(DATA = map(DATA, add_compute_state)) |>
  mutate(SUMMARY = map(DATA, summary_per_operation)) |>
  mutate(SUMMARY.PLOT = map(SUMMARY, plot_summary_per_operation)) |>
  mutate(SUMMARY.TIME.PLOT = map(DATA, plot_total_time_per_operation)) |>
  mutate(SUMMARY.COMBINED = map2(SUMMARY.PLOT, SUMMARY.TIME.PLOT, `|`)) |>
  mutate(DATA.AGG = map(DATA, do_the_reference_aggregation, 100)) |>
  # tradicional ST view
  mutate(ST = map(DATA, our_st_plot)) |>  
  mutate(ST.AGG = map(DATA.AGG, \(x) do_the_viz(x, has.summary = TRUE))) -> df

library(purrr)
pdf("plots.pdf", width = 10, height = 8)

df |>
  select(ST, ST.AGG, SUMMARY.COMBINED) |>
  pwalk(function(ST, ST.AGG, SUMMARY.COMBINED) {

    page <- (ST / ST.AGG) | SUMMARY.COMBINED
    print(page)

  })

dev.off()
#+end_src

#+RESULTS:

*** The aggregation framework (starvz-inspired)
**** integrateStepFunc
#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
source("integrateStepFunc.R")
#+end_src

#+RESULTS:

**** StarVZ functions copied "as is"
#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
integrate.stepfunc.Rcpp <- function(inter, b, f) integrateStepFunc(inter, c(-Inf, b, Inf), c(0, f, 0))

getBreaks <- function(dfv = NULL) {
  if (is.null(dfv)) {
    return(NULL)
  }
  breaks <- c(dfv$Start, dfv$End[length(dfv$End)])
  return(breaks)
}

getSlices <- function(dfv = NULL, step = 100) {
  tstart <- dfv %>%
    .$Start %>%
    min()
  tend <- (dfv %>% .$End %>% max())
  # TODO: Explain how we ignore the last slice if tend is not multiple
  # of step. This will make us ignore all behavior from the beginning
  # of that last slice until tend. This is unimportant for visualization
  # purposes but it can be important for stats. On that case, replace
  # the second argument by =tend+step= to make sure all data is considered.
  slices <- c(seq(0, tend, step), tend)
  return(slices)
}

remyTimeIntegration <- function(dfv = NULL, slices = NULL) {
  if (is.null(dfv)) {
    return(NULL)
  }
  if (is.null(slices)) {
    return(NULL)
  }

  # Define breaks
  breaks <- getBreaks(dfv)

  # Define values on breaks
  values <- dfv$Value

  result <- integrate.stepfunc.Rcpp(slices, breaks, values)

  return(result)
}

remyTimeIntegrationPrep <- function(dfv = NULL, myStep = 100) {
  if (is.null(dfv)) {
    return(NULL)
  }
  if (nrow(dfv) == 0) {
    return(NULL)
  }
  mySlices <- getSlices(dfv, step = myStep)
  tibble(Slice = mySlices, Value = c(remyTimeIntegration(dfv, slices = mySlices), 0) / myStep)
}
#+end_src

#+RESULTS:

**** NEW StarVZ adapted functions so they can be faster

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
do_the_aggregation <- function(df, step_width) {
  df |>
  select(ResourceId = Container, Task = Value, Start, End) |>
    arrange(ResourceId, Task, Start) |>
    group_by(ResourceId, Task) |>
    reframe({
      # Capture original Start/End before tibble() column shadowing can occur
      s <- Start
      e <- End
      bind_rows(
        tibble(Start = s, End = e, Active = 1),
        tibble(Start = e, End = lead(s), Active = 0) |> filter(!is.na(End)),
        tibble(Start = 0, End = first(s), Active = 0)
      )
    }) |>
    rename(Value = Active) |>
    arrange(ResourceId, Task, Start, End) |>
    group_by(ResourceId, Task) |>
    do(remyTimeIntegrationPrep(., myStep = step_width)) |>
    mutate(Start = Slice,
           End = lead(Slice),
           Duration = End - Start) |>
    ungroup() |>
    na.omit() 
}
#+end_src

#+RESULTS:

**** The reference aggregation

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
do_the_reference_aggregation <- function(df, nb_intervals) {
  df |> pull(Start) |> min() -> t.start
  df |> pull(End) |> max() -> t.end
  step_width = (t.end-t.start)/nb_intervals
  df |>
    do_the_aggregation(step_width) |>
    # make it has the same columns for our do_the_viz fun
    mutate(Slice = round(Slice / step_width)) |>
    rename(Container = ResourceId,
           Value = Task,
           Percent = Value,
           StartTS = Start, # Start of the timeslice (TS)
           EndTS = End,     # End of the timeslice (TS)
           DurationTS = Duration) |> # Duration of the timeslice (TS)
    mutate(Time.Sum = Percent * DurationTS)
}
#+end_src

#+RESULTS:

**** Plot function (do-the-viz)

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
library(patchwork)
do_the_viz <- function(df, has.summary = "Both")
{
  df |>
    rename(Rank = Container) -> df
  
  # Prep Y labels
  df |>
    distinct(Rank) |>
    arrange(Rank) |>
    mutate(Position = 0:(n()-1)) |>
    mutate(Label = Position) -> yconfm
  
  df |>
    filter(Time.Sum != 0) |>
    group_by(Rank, Slice, StartTS, EndTS, DurationTS, Value) |>
    summarize(Time.Sum = sum(Time.Sum), .groups="drop_last") |>
    ungroup(Value) |>
    arrange(Value) |>
    mutate(TaskHeight = Time.Sum / DurationTS) |>
    mutate(TaskPosition = cumsum(TaskHeight) - TaskHeight) |>
    left_join(yconfm, by="Rank") |>
    ggplot() +
    scale_y_continuous(
      breaks = yconfm$Position,
      labels = yconfm$Label
    ) +    
    geom_rect(alpha=.5, aes(
      fill = Value,
      xmin = StartTS,
      xmax = EndTS,
      ymin = Position + TaskPosition,
      ymax = Position + (TaskPosition + TaskHeight)
    )) +
    my_style() +
    theme(axis.title.x = element_blank(),
          axis.text.x = element_blank()) +
    ylab("Rank [index]") +
    xlab("Time [seconds]") -> p

# summary plot
  df |>
    filter(Time.Sum != 0) |>
    group_by(Slice, StartTS, EndTS, DurationTS, Value) |>
    summarize(N=n(), Time.Sum = sum(Time.Sum), .groups="drop_last") |>
    ungroup(Value) |>
    arrange(Value) |>
    mutate(TaskHeight = Time.Sum / (DurationTS * N)) |>
    mutate(TaskPosition = cumsum(TaskHeight) - TaskHeight) |>
    ggplot() +
    coord_cartesian(ylim=c(0,1)) +
    geom_rect(alpha=.5, aes(
      fill = Value,
      xmin = StartTS,
      xmax = EndTS,
      ymin = TaskPosition,
      ymax = (TaskPosition + TaskHeight)
    )) +
    my_style() +
    theme(legend.position="none") +
    ylab("Load [%]") +
    xlab("Time [seconds]") -> p.summary
 
  if (has.summary == "Both") {
    p / p.summary + plot_layout(heights = c(1, 0.15))
  }else if (has.summary == "Summary") {
    p.summary + theme(legend.justification = "left", legend.position="top")
  }else{
    p
  }
}
#+end_src

        MPI_Irecv  = "#4DAF4A",  # Set1 green
        MPI_Isend  = "#E41A1C",  # Set1 red
        MPI_Waitall = "#377EB8", # Set1 blue
        Compute     = "#FFD92F"  # yellow        
      )
    ),
    theme_bw(base_size = 16),
    theme(legend.position="top"),
    theme(
      legend.title = element_blank(),
      plot.margin = unit(c(0, 0, 0, 0), "cm"),
      legend.spacing = unit(1, "mm"),
      legend.justification = "left",
      legend.box.spacing = unit(0, "pt"),

      axis.text.x = element_text(angle=45, vjust=1, hjust=1)
    ))
}

#+RESULTS:

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
plot_summary_per_operation <- function(df) {

  ggplot(df, aes(x = Value)) +

    # min → max range
    geom_linerange(aes(ymin = min, ymax = max),
                   linewidth = 0.6, alpha = 0.5) +

    # interquartile range
    geom_linerange(aes(ymin = p25, ymax = p75),
                   linewidth = 3) +

    # median
    geom_point(aes(y = median), size = 3, shape = 21, fill = "white") +

    # p90 and p99 markers
    geom_point(aes(y = p90), shape = 17, size = 2) +
    geom_point(aes(y = p99), shape = 18, size = 2) +

    # sample size label
    geom_text(aes(y = max, label = paste0("n=", n)),
              vjust = -0.5, size = 3) +

#    scale_y_log10() +

    labs(
      x = "Operation",
      y = "Duration",
    ) +

    theme_bw()
}
#+end_src

#+RESULTS:
**** Plot total time per operation
#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
plot_total_time_per_operation <- function(df) {

  df |>
    group_by(Value) |>
    summarise(total_duration = sum(Duration, na.rm = TRUE),
              .groups = "drop") |>
    ggplot(aes(x = Value, y = total_duration, fill = Value)) +
    
    geom_col(width = 0.7) +
    
    geom_text(aes(label = scales::scientific(total_duration)),
              vjust = -0.3, size = 3) +
    
    labs(
      x = "Operation",
      y = "Total Duration",
    ) +
    
    theme_bw() +
    theme(legend.position = "none")
}
#+end_src

tibble(FILE = dir_ls(THE.DIR, pattern="*.csv")) |>
  mutate(KEY = str_remove(basename(FILE), "\\.csv$")) |>  
  mutate(DATA = map(FILE, our_read_function)) |>
  mutate(DATA = map(DATA, add_compute_state)) |>
  mutate(SUMMARY = map(DATA, summary_per_operation)) |>
  mutate(SUMMARY.PLOT = map(SUMMARY, plot_summary_per_operation)) |>
  mutate(SUMMARY.TIME.PLOT = map(DATA, plot_total_time_per_operation)) |>
  mutate(SUMMARY.COMBINED = map2(SUMMARY.PLOT, SUMMARY.TIME.PLOT, `|`)) |>
  mutate(DATA.AGG = map(DATA, do_the_reference_aggregation, 100)) |>
  # tradicional ST view
  mutate(ST = map(DATA, our_st_plot)) |>  
  mutate(ST.AGG = map(DATA.AGG, \(x) do_the_viz(x, has.summary = "Summary"))) -> df

** 2026-04-26 Códigos para relatório
*** Custo de Comunicação vs. Estratégia de Particionamento
#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
                                        # Carregar bibliotecas
library(ggplot2)
library(tidyr)

                                        # Definir os dados
P <- seq(1, 1000, by = 10) # Número de processadores
L <- 1 # Comprimento do lado normalizado

                                        # Fórmulas da Área de Superfície Interna
area_1d <- 2 * (P - 1) * L^2
area_2d <- 4 * (sqrt(P) - 1) * L^2
area_3d <- 6 * (P^(1/3) - 1) * L^2

                                        # Criar um data frame e converter para o formato longo (long format) para o ggplot
df <- data.frame(Processadores = P, 
                 `Fatias` = area_1d, 
                 `Colunas` = area_2d, 
                 `Blocos` = area_3d)

df_long <- pivot_longer(df, cols = -Processadores, 
                        names_to = "Tipo_de_Particionamento", 
                        values_to = "Area_de_Fronteira")

                                        # Gerar o gráfico
ggplot(df_long, aes(x = Processadores, y = Area_de_Fronteira, color = Tipo_de_Particionamento)) +
  geom_line(size = 1.2) +
  labs(title = "Custo de Comunicação vs. Estratégia de Particionamento",
       subtitle = "Comparando Decomposição 1D, 2D e 3D para um Cubo",
       x = "Número de Processadores (P)",
       y = "Área de Fronteira Interna\n(Volume de Comunicação\nem itens comunicados)",
       color = "Estratégia") +
  theme_minimal() +
  coord_cartesian(ylim=c(0, 200)) +
  scale_color_manual(values = c("red", "blue", "darkgreen")) +
  theme(
    plot.margin = unit(c(0, 0, 0, 0), "cm"),
    legend.spacing = unit(1, "mm"),
    legend.position = "top",
    legend.justification = "left",
    legend.box.spacing = unit(0, "pt"),
    legend.box.margin = margin(0, 0, 0, 0)
  )  
#+end_src

#+RESULTS:
*** Visualização com Pyvista das estratégias de particionamento
**** Inspirador (3D)
#+begin_src python :eval no
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
from mpl_toolkits.mplot3d.art3d import Poly3DCollection
import itertools


def cube_faces(x, y, z, s):
    """
    Create the 6 faces of a cube located at (x,y,z)
    with side length s.
    """
    vertices = [
        (x, y, z),
        (x + s, y, z),
        (x + s, y + s, z),
        (x, y + s, z),
        (x, y, z + s),
        (x + s, y, z + s),
        (x + s, y + s, z + s),
        (x, y + s, z + s),
    ]

    faces = [
        [vertices[i] for i in [0, 1, 2, 3]],  # bottom
        [vertices[i] for i in [4, 5, 6, 7]],  # top
        [vertices[i] for i in [0, 1, 5, 4]],  # front
        [vertices[i] for i in [2, 3, 7, 6]],  # back
        [vertices[i] for i in [1, 2, 6, 5]],  # right
        [vertices[i] for i in [0, 3, 7, 4]],  # left
    ]

    return faces


# Create figure
fig = plt.figure(figsize=(8, 8))
ax = fig.add_subplot(111, projection="3d")

# Parameters
n = 3          # 3x3x3 grid
size = 1.0     # cube size
gap = 0.15     # spacing between cubes

# Light blue-gray color
face_color = "#cfd8dc"

# Generate cubes
for i, j, k in itertools.product(range(n), repeat=3):
    x = i * (size + gap)
    y = j * (size + gap)
    z = k * (size + gap)

    cube = Poly3DCollection(
        cube_faces(x, y, z, size),
        facecolors=face_color,
        edgecolors="black",
        linewidths=0.8,
        alpha=1.0
    )

    ax.add_collection3d(cube)

# Adjust plot limits
extent = n * size + (n - 1) * gap
ax.set_xlim(0, extent)
ax.set_ylim(0, extent)
ax.set_zlim(0, extent)

# Keep proportions equal
ax.set_box_aspect([1, 1, 1])

# Clean schematic look
ax.axis("off")

# Camera angle
ax.view_init(elev=22, azim=35)

plt.tight_layout()
plt.show()
#+end_src
**** Pyvista 1D

#+begin_src python
import pyvista as pv

n = 64
gap = 0.01
size = 1.0

pv.global_theme.transparent_background = True
plotter = pv.Plotter(off_screen=True, border=False, window_size=[2000, 2000])
plotter.hide_axes()
plotter.remove_bounding_box()

for i in range(n):
    # Each slab is very thin (size/n)
    x_start = i * (size/n + gap)
    slab = pv.Box(bounds=(x_start, x_start + size/n, 0, size, 0, size))
    plotter.add_mesh(slab, color="#f5f7f8", edge_color="black", show_edges=True)

# Perfect Centering Logic
xyz_max = (n - 1) * gap + size
center = (xyz_max / 2, xyz_max / 2, xyz_max / 2)
d = xyz_max * 2.5 # Adjust distance to ensure the whole cube fits
plotter.camera_position = [(center[0] + d, center[1] + d, center[2] + d), center, (0, 0, 1)]

# Export to PDF
plotter.screenshot("partition_1d.png")

from PIL import Image
def crop_transparent_png(input_file, output_pdf):
    # Open the image
    img = Image.open(input_file)
    
    # getbbox() finds the bounding box of non-zero (non-transparent) data
    bbox = img.getbbox()
    
    if bbox:
        # Crop the image to the bounding box
        cropped_img = img.crop(bbox)
        
        # Convert to RGB (PDF doesn't support transparency well) 
        # and save as PDF
        cropped_img.convert("RGB").save(output_pdf)
        print(f"Cropped and saved: {output_pdf}")
    else:
        print("Image is completely transparent!")

# Apply to your file
crop_transparent_png("partition_1d.png", "partition_1d.png")
#+end_src

#+begin_src python
import pyvista as pv
import itertools
import os
from PIL import Image

# Configurações (ex: 4x4 = 16 colunas)
n = 8
gap = 0.01
size = 1.0

pv.global_theme.transparent_background = True
plotter = pv.Plotter(off_screen=True, border=False, window_size=[2000, 2000])
plotter.hide_axes()
plotter.remove_bounding_box()

for i, j in itertools.product(range(n), range(n)):
    x_start = i * (size/n + gap)
    y_start = j * (size/n + gap)
    
    # Colunas longas no eixo Z
    column = pv.Box(bounds=(x_start, x_start + size/n, 
                            y_start, y_start + size/n, 
                            0, size))
    
    plotter.add_mesh(column, color="#f5f7f8", edge_color="black", show_edges=True)

# Perfect Centering Logic
xyz_max = (n - 1) * gap + size
center = (xyz_max / 2, xyz_max / 2, xyz_max / 2)
d = xyz_max * 2.5 # Adjust distance to ensure the whole cube fits
plotter.camera_position = [(center[0] + d, center[1] + d, center[2] + d), center, (0, 0, 1)]

# Export to PDF
plotter.screenshot("partition_2d.png")

    x_s = i * (size/n + gap)
    y_s = j * (size/n + gap)
    z_s = k * (size/n + gap)
    block = pv.Box(bounds=(x_s, x_s + size/n, y_s, y_s + size/n, z_s, z_s + size/n))

*** Pyvista ghost-cells
**** Apenas as ghost-cells

#+begin_src python
import pyvista as pv
import itertools

# Configuração
n = 4          # 3x3x3 para não poluir visualmente
size = 1.0     # tamanho do núcleo local
ghost = 0.1   # espessura da camada de ghost cells
gap = 0.12      # gap maior para ver os blocos isolados


pv.global_theme.transparent_background = True
plotter = pv.Plotter(off_screen=True, border=False, window_size=[2000, 2000])
plotter.hide_axes()
plotter.remove_bounding_box()
# Generate Blocks
for i, j, k in itertools.product(range(n), repeat=3):
    # Posição base
    x_s = i * (size + 2*ghost + gap)
    y_s = j * (size + 2*ghost + gap)
    z_s = k * (size + 2*ghost + gap)
    
    # 1. O NÚCLEO (Dados reais do processo)
    core = pv.Box(bounds=(x_s + ghost, x_s + ghost + size, 
                          y_s + ghost, y_s + ghost + size, 
                          z_s + ghost, z_s + ghost + size))
    
    # 2. AS GHOST CELLS (A "casca" que envolve o núcleo)
    # Criamos um cubo ligeiramente maior que engloba o núcleo
    shell = pv.Box(bounds=(x_s, x_s + size + 2*ghost, 
                           y_s, y_s + size + 2*ghost, 
                           z_s, z_s + size + 2*ghost))
    
    # Adiciona a casca (transparente)
    plotter.add_mesh(shell, color="orange", opacity=0.3, show_edges=True, edge_color="red")
    
    # Adiciona o núcleo (sólido)
    plotter.add_mesh(core, color="#cfd8dc", opacity=1.0, show_edges=True, edge_color="black")

# Ajuste de Câmera para ver a quina
xyz_max = n * (size + 2*ghost + gap)
center = (xyz_max/2, xyz_max/2, xyz_max/2)
d = xyz_max * 1.8
plotter.camera_position = [(center[0]+d, center[1]+d, center[2]+d), center, (0,0,1)]

# Export to PDF
plotter.screenshot("ghost_cells.png")

from PIL import Image
def crop_transparent_png(input_file, output_pdf):
    # Open the image
    img = Image.open(input_file)
    
    # getbbox() finds the bounding box of non-zero (non-transparent) data
    bbox = img.getbbox()
    
    if bbox:
        # Crop the image to the bounding box
        cropped_img = img.crop(bbox)
        
        # Convert to RGB (PDF doesn't support transparency well) 
        # and save as PDF
        cropped_img.convert("RGB").save(output_pdf)
        print(f"Cropped and saved: {output_pdf}")
    else:
        print("Image is completely transparent!")

# Apply to your file
crop_transparent_png("ghost_cells.png", "ghost_cells.png")
#+end_src

**** Bordas comunicantes
#+begin_src python
import pyvista as pv
import itertools

# Configuração
n = 4          # 3x3x3 para não poluir visualmente
s = 1.0     # tamanho do núcleo local
g = 0.1   # espessura da camada de ghost cells
gap = 0.12      # gap maior para ver os blocos isolados

pv.global_theme.transparent_background = True
plotter = pv.Plotter(off_screen=True, border=False, window_size=[2000, 2000])
plotter.hide_axes()
plotter.remove_bounding_box()
# Generate Blocks
for i, j, k in itertools.product(range(n), repeat=3):
    # Posição central do bloco i,j,k
    x = i * (s + gap)
    y = j * (s + gap)
    z = k * (s + gap)

    # 1. O CORE (Dados Locais)
    core = pv.Box(bounds=(x, x+s, y, y+s, z, z+s))
    plotter.add_mesh(core, color="#cfd8dc", edge_color="black", show_edges=True)

    # 2. ADICIONAR GHOST CELLS APENAS ONDE HÁ VIZINHOS
    # Ghost Cell em X (Direita)
    if i < n - 1:
        ghost_x = pv.Box(bounds=(x+s, x+s+g, y, y+s, z, z+s))
        plotter.add_mesh(ghost_x, color="orange", opacity=0.6, edge_color="red", show_edges=True)
    
    # Ghost Cell em Y (Fundo)
    if j < n - 1:
        ghost_y = pv.Box(bounds=(x, x+s, y+s, y+s+g, z, z+s))
        plotter.add_mesh(ghost_y, color="green", opacity=0.6, edge_color="darkgreen", show_edges=True)

    # Ghost Cell em Z (Topo)
    if k < n - 1:
        ghost_z = pv.Box(bounds=(x, x+s, y, y+s, z+s, z+s+g))
        plotter.add_mesh(ghost_z, color="blue", opacity=0.6, edge_color="darkblue", show_edges=True)

    
# Ajuste de Câmera para ver a quina
xyz_max = n * (s + 2*g + gap)
center = (xyz_max/2, xyz_max/2, xyz_max/2)
d = xyz_max * 1.8
plotter.camera_position = [(center[0]+d, center[1]+d, center[2]+d), center, (0,0,1)]

# Export to PDF
plotter.screenshot("ghost_cells-comm.png")

from PIL import Image
def crop_transparent_png(input_file, output_pdf):
    # Open the image
    img = Image.open(input_file)
    
    # getbbox() finds the bounding box of non-zero (non-transparent) data
    bbox = img.getbbox()
    
    if bbox:
        # Crop the image to the bounding box
        cropped_img = img.crop(bbox)
        
        # Convert to RGB (PDF doesn't support transparency well) 
        # and save as PDF
        cropped_img.convert("RGB").save(output_pdf)
        print(f"Cropped and saved: {output_pdf}")
    else:
        print("Image is completely transparent!")

# Apply to your file
crop_transparent_png("ghost_cells-comm.png", "ghost_cells-comm.png")
#+end_src

** 2026-05-17 CARLA Article
*** How to run a simulation
#+begin_src shell :results output :exports both :tangle ../script.sh :tangle-mode (identity #o755) :shebang "#!/usr/bin/bash"
#./simgrid-config/compile_platform.sh
export PLATFORM_NUM_HOSTS=6
seq 0 $((PLATFORM_NUM_HOSTS - 1)) | sed 's/^/host-/' > simgrid-config/hostfile.txt
export PLATFORM_NET_LAT="22.7us"
export PLATFORM_NET_BW="10Gbps"
export PROBLEM_SIZE=128
nix run .#run-simgrid-platform-cuda -- $PLATFORM_NUM_HOSTS $PLATFORM_NET_BW $PLATFORM_NET_LAT \
      --size-x=${PROBLEM_SIZE} \
      --size-y=${PROBLEM_SIZE} \
      --size-z=${PROBLEM_SIZE} \
      --absorption=2 \
      --dx=1e-1 \
      --dy=1e-1 \
      --dz=1e-1 \
      --dt=1e-6 \
      --time-max=1e-3 \
      --output-file=./validation/predicted.dc 2>&1 | tee sim.log
#+end_src

#+RESULTS:
: /home/schnorr/svn/spadotto/distributed-cube-average
*** DoE Case studies
**** *1. CPU Cluster: Communication Masking Progression (cei, 10 Gbps)*

Compare the 256^3 (~75% compute load) and 512^3 (~87% compute load)
executions on the *cei* cluster. This directly demonstrates the
O(n3)O(n^3) O(n3) volume vs. O(n2)O(n^2) O(n2) boundary growth argument
in action, using the Gantt and load charts as evidence.

*cei* (cpu-only, openmp)

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
options(crayon.enabled=FALSE)
library(tidyverse)
crossing(
  size = c(64, 128, 256, 512), # PROBLEM_SIZE
  hosts = c(8, 16, 32, 64),    # PLATFORM_NUM_HOSTS
  speed = c(0.010, 0.025, 0.04, 0.05, 0.1, 1, 2.5, 10) # in Gbps, #PLATFORM_NET_BW
)

#+RESULTS:

#+end_example

**** *2. GPU Cluster: The Network Bottleneck (poti, 1 Gbps)*

Show how compute load stays stuck at ~20% regardless of problem size
(128^3, 256^3, 512^3) when the RTX 4070 is paired with a Gigabit
network. This is a compelling negative result — it motivates
simulation and illustrates that GPU throughput can *outrun* the
interconnect.

**** *3. Simulated Network Upgrade: 1 Gbps → 10 Gbps → 100 Gbps*

Using the *poti* calibration, trace the progression of compute
load from ~20% (real) to ~65–80% (10 Gbps simulated) to >90% (100 Gbps
simulated) at 512^3. This is arguably the strongest story in the paper:
simulation as a practical tool for capacity planning.

**** *4. Partitioning Topology: Block vs. Slices*

Contrast the 8-worker {2,2,2} block decomposition against a 5-worker
{5,1,1} slices decomposition (which fell below the single-node
baseline). This makes the prime-process-count pitfall concrete and
ties back to the theoretical boundary formula.
*** The Masking Effectiveness Analysis
**** Steps
***** 1. Script to calculate Masking Effectiveness for every run
:PROPERTIES:
:header-args: :tangle "me.R" :tangle-mode (identity #o755) :shebang "#!/usr/bin/Rscript"
:END:
****** Functions
******* Read

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
our_read_function <- function(f) {
  read_csv(f,
           show_col_types=FALSE,
           progress=FALSE) |>
    mutate(Container = as.integer(gsub("rank-?", "", Container))) |>
    mutate(Value = str_trim(gsub("^\\s*PMPI_", "MPI_", str_trim(Value)))) |>    
    mutate(Value = as.factor(Value)) |>
    filter(Value %in% c("MPI_Irecv", "MPI_Isend", "MPI_Waitall")) |>
    mutate(Value = factor(Value, levels=c("MPI_Irecv", "MPI_Isend", "MPI_Waitall"))) -> df
# Keep only the part that interest us
# Highly dependent on parallel design
  core_start <- df |>    
    filter(Value == "MPI_Irecv") |>    
    pull(Start) |>    
    min()    
  core_end <- df |>    
    filter(Value == "MPI_Waitall") |>    
    pull(End) |>    
    max()    
  df <- df |>    
    filter(Start < core_end) |>    
    filter(End > core_start) |>    
    mutate(Start = pmax(Start, core_start), End = pmin(End, core_end), Duration = End - Start) |>
    select(Container, Value, Start, End)
# Return the data frame
  return(df)
}
#+end_src

#+RESULTS:

******* Compute

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
add_compute_state <- function(df) {

  compute <- df |>
    arrange(Container, Start) |>
    group_by(Container) |>
    mutate(next_start = lead(Start)) |>
    filter(!is.na(next_start), next_start > End) |>
    transmute(
      Container,
      Start = End,
      End = next_start,
      Value = factor("Compute", levels = c(levels(df$Value), "Compute"))
    )

  bind_rows(df, compute) |>
    arrange(Container, Start) |>
    ungroup()
}
#+end_src

#+RESULTS:

****** Read and compute

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
options(crayon.enabled=FALSE)
suppressMessages(library(tidyverse))
suppressMessages(library(fs))

tibble(
  FILE="dc.state.csv"
) |>
#  mutate(Order = str_extract(FILE, "(?<=order-)\\d+") |> as.integer()) |>
#  left_join(read_csv(paste0(BASE_DIR, "poti-doe.csv"), progress=FALSE, show_col_types=FALSE), by="Order") |>
  mutate(DATA = map(FILE, our_read_function)) |>
  mutate(DATA = map(DATA, add_compute_state)) -> df
#+end_src


#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
df |>
  select(-FILE) |>
  unnest(DATA) |>
  mutate(Type = ifelse(Value == "Compute", "Compute", "Communication")) |>
  filter(Type == "Communication") |>
#  group_by(Order, size, hosts, speed, Container) |>
  group_by(Container) |>  
  summarize(
    Makespan = max(End) - min(Start),
    Duration = sum(End-Start),
    .groups="drop_last") |>
  print() |>
  summarize(
    Communication = sum(Duration) / sum(Makespan),
    Masking.Effectiveness = 1 - Communication,
    .groups="drop_last") |>
  print() |>
  write_csv("me.csv")
#+end_src

***** 2. Run the script for all cases
****** Sequential
#+begin_src shell :results output :exports both :tangle no
for i in $(find swr-poti | grep order- | grep dc.state.csv)
do
    pushd $(dirname $i)
    ../../../../../me.R
    popd
done
#+end_src
****** Parallel
#+begin_src shell :results output :exports both
find swr-weak-scalability-new-17 -type f -path '*order-*dc.state.csv' | \
parallel --will-cite -j 4 '
    cd "$(dirname {})" &&
    ../../../../../me.R < /dev/null
'
#+end_src

#poti
BASE.DIR <- "swr-all-after-arch-check-2/run-784330/"
BASE.DIR <- "swr-poti/run-784314/"
tupi
BASE.DIR <- "swr-tupi/run-784327/"
#cei
#BASE.DIR <- "swr-cei/run-784319/"

#BASE.DIR <- "swr-tsubasa/run-784320/"

DOE.BASE.DIR <- paste0(BASE.DIR, "distributed-cube-average/tupi-doe/")

tibble(
  FILE=dir_ls(BASE.DIR,
              recurse=TRUE,
              regexp="me.csv")
) |>
  mutate(Order = str_extract(FILE, "(?<=order-)\\d+") |> as.integer()) |>
  left_join(read_csv(paste0(DOE.BASE.DIR, "tupi-doe.csv"), progress=FALSE, show_col_types=FALSE), by="Order") |>
  mutate(ME = map(FILE, function(f) {
    read_csv(f, progress=FALSE, show_col_types=FALSE)
  })) |>
  unnest(ME)  |>
  select(-FILE) |>
  select(-Communication) |>
  mutate(speed = as.factor(speed)) |>
  mutate(hosts = as.factor(hosts)) |>
  mutate(size = as.factor(size)) |>
  write_csv("masking.csv", progress=FALSE) |>
  ggplot(aes(
    color = hosts, group= hosts,
    x = speed,
    y = Masking.Effectiveness)) +
  geom_line(alpha=.5) +
  geom_point() +
  ylim(0, 1) +
  facet_wrap(~size, nrow=1) +
  theme_bw(base_size=6) +
  scale_color_brewer(palette = "Set1", name = "Number of MPI ranks") +
 # scale_x_continuous(expand = c(0.01, 0)) +

  theme(
    plot.margin = unit(c(0, 0.2, 0, 0), "cm"),

    legend.box.margin = margin(0, 0, 0, 0),
    axis.text.x = element_text(angle = 45, hjust = 1)
  ) -> p

#+RESULTS:
**** Read everything

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
library(tidyverse)

# Your tibble
runs <- tribble(
  ~DIR,                                    ~TYPE,
  "swr-all-after-arch-check-2/run-784330/", "poti",
  "swr-poti/run-784314/",                   "poti",
  "swr-tupi/run-784327/",                   "tupi",
  "swr-cei/run-784319/",                    "cei",
  "swr-tsubasa/run-784320/",                "tsubasa"
)

read_me_files <- function(dir, type) {
  # Determine the doe subdirectory name based on type
  doe_dir <- str_glue("{dir}distributed-cube-average/{type}-doe")

  # Find all me.csv files and extract their order
  me_files <- fs::dir_ls(doe_dir, regexp = "order-[0-9]+/me\\.csv$", recurse = TRUE)

  # Read all me.csv files, tagging each with its order number
  me_data <- me_files |>
    map(read_csv, show_col_types = FALSE, progress=FALSE) |>
    list_rbind(names_to = "path") |>
    mutate(
      order = as.integer(str_extract(path, "(?<=order-)\\d+")),
      DIR   = dir,
      TYPE  = type
    ) |>
    select(-path)

  # Read the DoE file
  doe_file <- str_glue("{doe_dir}/{type}-doe.csv")
  doe_data <- read_csv(doe_file, show_col_types = FALSE, progress=FALSE)

  # Left-join me data with DoE on order
  left_join(me_data, doe_data, by = c("order" = "Order"))
}

# Apply across all runs and bind results
runs |>
  rowwise() |>
  slice(1) |>
  reframe(read_me_files(DIR, TYPE)) |>
  mutate(TYPE = factor(TYPE, levels=c("cei", "tsubasa", "poti", "tupi"))) |>
  select(-DIR) |>
  select(TYPE, order, size, hosts, speed, Masking.Effectiveness) |>
  write_csv("all-final.csv")
#+end_src

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
# ============================================================
# Masking Effectiveness — GPU heatmap (poti + tupi), article style
# ============================================================

options(crayon.enabled = FALSE)
library(tidyverse)
library(ggplot2)

# ── 0. Configuration ─────────────────────────────────────────
DATA_FILE <- "all-final.csv"

# ── 1. Load data ─────────────────────────────────────────────
df <- read_csv(DATA_FILE, show_col_types = FALSE) |>
  filter(TYPE %in% c("poti", "tupi")) |>
  mutate(
    TYPE  = factor(TYPE, levels = c("poti", "tupi")),
    size  = factor(size),
    hosts = factor(hosts),
    speed = factor(speed)
  )

# ── 2. Plot ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
p <- df |>
  ggplot(aes(x = speed, y = hosts, fill = Masking.Effectiveness)) +
  geom_tile(color = "white", linewidth = 0.2) +
  scale_fill_viridis_c(
    name   = "Masking Effectiveness",
    limits = c(0, 1),
    breaks = seq(0, 1, by = 0.2),
    guide  = guide_colorbar(
      title.position = "top",
      barwidth       = unit(3, "cm"),
      barheight      = unit(0.2, "cm")
    )
  ) +
  facet_grid(size ~ TYPE, labeller = label_both) +
  labs(
    x = "Network Speed (Gbps)",
    y = "Number of MPI Ranks"
  ) +
  theme_bw(base_size = 6) +
  theme(
    plot.margin          = unit(c(0, 0.2, 0, 0), "cm"),
    legend.spacing       = unit(0.1, "mm"),
    panel.grid           = element_blank(),
    legend.position      = "top",
    legend.direction     = "horizontal",
    legend.justification = "left",
    legend.key.size      = unit(0.2, "cm"),
    legend.box.spacing   = unit(0, "pt"),
    legend.box.margin    = margin(0, 0, 0, 0),
    strip.text           = element_text(size = 6),
    axis.text.x          = element_text(angle = 45, hjust = 1),
    panel.spacing        = unit(0.2, "cm")
  )

# One-column article width: 8.5cm wide, compact height
ggsave("masking_heatmap_gpu.pdf", plot = p, width = 8.5, height = 9, units = "cm")
ggsave("masking_heatmap_gpu.png", plot = p, width = 8.5, height = 9, units = "cm", dpi = 300)
cat("Plot saved to masking_heatmap_gpu.pdf and .png\n")

read_me_files <- function(dir, type) {
  # Determine the doe subdirectory name based on type
  doe_dir <- str_glue("{dir}distributed-cube-average/{type}-weak-scalability")

  # Find all me.csv files and extract their order
  me_files <- fs::dir_ls(doe_dir, regexp = "order-[0-9]+/me\\.csv$", recurse = TRUE)

  # Read all me.csv files, tagging each with its order number
  me_data <- me_files |>
    map(read_csv, show_col_types = FALSE, progress=FALSE) |>
    list_rbind(names_to = "path") |>
    mutate(
      order = as.integer(str_extract(path, "(?<=order-)\\d+")),
      DIR   = dir,
      TYPE  = type
    ) |>
    select(-path)

  # Read the DoE file
  doe_file <- str_glue("{doe_dir}/{type}-weak-scalability.csv")
  doe_data <- read_csv(doe_file, show_col_types = FALSE, progress=FALSE)

  # Left-join me data with DoE on order
  left_join(me_data, doe_data, by = c("order" = "Order"))
}

# Apply across all runs and bind results
runs |>
  rowwise() |>
  slice(1) |>
  reframe(read_me_files(DIR, TYPE)) |>
  mutate(TYPE = factor(TYPE, levels=c("cei", "tsubasa", "poti", "tupi"))) |>
  select(-DIR) |>
  select(-Communication) |>
  write_csv("swr-weak-scalability.csv", progress=FALSE) |>
  print()

read_me_files <- function(dir, type) {

  doe_dir <- str_glue("{dir}distributed-cube-average/{type}-weak-scalability-new")

    map(read_csv, show_col_types = FALSE, progress=FALSE) |>
    list_rbind(names_to = "path") |>
    mutate(
      order = as.integer(str_extract(path, "(?<=order-)\\d+")),
      DIR   = dir,
      TYPE  = type
    ) |>
    select(-path)

  # Read the DoE file
  doe_file <- str_glue("{doe_dir}/{type}-weak-scalability-new.csv")

options(crayon.enabled=FALSE)
library(tidyverse)

# Your tibble
runs <- tribble(
  ~DIR,                                    ~TYPE,
  "swr-weak-scalability-new-17/run-785720/", "poti",
)

read_me_files <- function(dir, type) {
  # Determine the doe subdirectory name based on type
  doe_dir <- str_glue("{dir}distributed-cube-average/{type}-weak-scalability-new-17")

  # Find all me.csv files and extract their order
  me_files <- fs::dir_ls(doe_dir, regexp = "order-[0-9]+/me\\.csv$", recurse = TRUE)

  # Read all me.csv files, tagging each with its order number
  me_data <- me_files |>
    map(read_csv, show_col_types = FALSE, progress=FALSE) |>
    list_rbind(names_to = "path") |>
    mutate(
      order = as.integer(str_extract(path, "(?<=order-)\\d+")),
      DIR   = dir,
      TYPE  = type
    )# |>
#    select(-path)

  # Read the DoE file
  doe_file <- str_glue("{doe_dir}/{type}-weak-scalability-new-17.csv")
  doe_data <- read_csv(doe_file, show_col_types = FALSE, progress=FALSE)

  # Left-join me data with DoE on order
  left_join(me_data, doe_data, by = c("order" = "Order"))
}

# Apply across all runs and bind results
runs |>
  rowwise() |>
  slice(1) |>
  reframe(read_me_files(DIR, TYPE)) |>
  mutate(TYPE = factor(TYPE, levels=c("cei", "tsubasa", "poti", "tupi"))) |>
 # select(-DIR) |>
  select(-Communication) |>
  write_csv("swr-weak-scalability-new-17.csv", progress=FALSE) |>
  print()
#+end_src

****** The aggregation framework (starvz-inspired)
******* integrateStepFunc
#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
source("integrateStepFunc.R")

#+RESULTS:

******* StarVZ functions copied "as is"
#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
integrate.stepfunc.Rcpp <- function(inter, b, f) integrateStepFunc(inter, c(-Inf, b, Inf), c(0, f, 0))

getBreaks <- function(dfv = NULL) {
  if (is.null(dfv)) {
    return(NULL)
  }
  breaks <- c(dfv$Start, dfv$End[length(dfv$End)])
  return(breaks)
}

getSlices <- function(dfv = NULL, step = 100) {
  tstart <- dfv %>%
    .$Start %>%
    min()
  tend <- (dfv %>% .$End %>% max())
  # TODO: Explain how we ignore the last slice if tend is not multiple
  # of step. This will make us ignore all behavior from the beginning
  # of that last slice until tend. This is unimportant for visualization
  # purposes but it can be important for stats. On that case, replace
  # the second argument by =tend+step= to make sure all data is considered.
  slices <- c(seq(0, tend, step), tend)
  return(slices)
}

remyTimeIntegration <- function(dfv = NULL, slices = NULL) {
  if (is.null(dfv)) {
    return(NULL)
  }
  if (is.null(slices)) {
    return(NULL)
  }

  # Define breaks
  breaks <- getBreaks(dfv)

  # Define values on breaks
  values <- dfv$Value

  result <- integrate.stepfunc.Rcpp(slices, breaks, values)

  return(result)
}

remyTimeIntegrationPrep <- function(dfv = NULL, myStep = 100) {
  if (is.null(dfv)) {
    return(NULL)
  }
  if (nrow(dfv) == 0) {
    return(NULL)
  }
  mySlices <- getSlices(dfv, step = myStep)
  tibble(Slice = mySlices, Value = c(remyTimeIntegration(dfv, slices = mySlices), 0) / myStep)
}
#+end_src

#+RESULTS:

******* NEW StarVZ adapted functions so they can be faster

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
do_the_aggregation <- function(df, step_width) {
  df |>
  select(ResourceId = Container, Task = Value, Start, End) |>
    arrange(ResourceId, Task, Start) |>
    group_by(ResourceId, Task) |>
    reframe({
      # Capture original Start/End before tibble() column shadowing can occur
      s <- Start
      e <- End
      bind_rows(
        tibble(Start = s, End = e, Active = 1),
        tibble(Start = e, End = lead(s), Active = 0) |> filter(!is.na(End)),
        tibble(Start = 0, End = first(s), Active = 0)
      )
    }) |>
    rename(Value = Active) |>
    arrange(ResourceId, Task, Start, End) |>
    group_by(ResourceId, Task) |>
    do(remyTimeIntegrationPrep(., myStep = step_width)) |>
    mutate(Start = Slice,
           End = lead(Slice),
           Duration = End - Start) |>
    ungroup() |>
    na.omit() 
}
#+end_src

#+RESULTS:

******* The reference aggregation

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
do_the_reference_aggregation <- function(df, nb_intervals) {
  df |> pull(Start) |> min() -> t.start
  df |> pull(End) |> max() -> t.end
  step_width = (t.end-t.start)/nb_intervals
  df |>
    do_the_aggregation(step_width) |>
    # make it has the same columns for our do_the_viz fun
    mutate(Slice = round(Slice / step_width)) |>
    rename(Container = ResourceId,
           Value = Task,
           Percent = Value,
           StartTS = Start, # Start of the timeslice (TS)
           EndTS = End,     # End of the timeslice (TS)
           DurationTS = Duration) |> # Duration of the timeslice (TS)
    mutate(Time.Sum = Percent * DurationTS)
}
#+end_src

#+RESULTS:

******* Plot function (do-the-viz)

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
library(patchwork)
do_the_viz <- function(df, has.summary = "Both")
{
  df |>
    rename(Rank = Container) -> df
  
  # Prep Y labels
  df |>
    distinct(Rank) |>
    arrange(Rank) |>
    mutate(Position = 0:(n()-1)) |>
    mutate(Label = Position) -> yconfm
  
  df |>
    filter(Time.Sum != 0) |>
    filter(Value %in% c("Compute", "MPI_Waitall")) |>
    group_by(Rank, Slice, StartTS, EndTS, DurationTS, Value) |>
    summarize(Time.Sum = sum(Time.Sum), .groups="drop_last") |>
    ungroup(Value) |>
    arrange(Value) |>
    mutate(TaskHeight = Time.Sum / DurationTS) |>
    mutate(TaskPosition = cumsum(TaskHeight) - TaskHeight) |>
    left_join(yconfm, by="Rank") |>
    ggplot() +
    scale_y_continuous(
      breaks = yconfm$Position,
      labels = yconfm$Label
    ) +    
    geom_rect(alpha=.5, aes(
      fill = Value,
      xmin = StartTS,
      xmax = EndTS,
      ymin = Position + TaskPosition,
      ymax = Position + (TaskPosition + TaskHeight)
    )) +
    my_style() +
    theme_bw(base_size=6) +
#    theme(axis.title.x = element_blank(),
#          axis.text.x = element_blank()) +
    ylab("Rank [index]") +
    xlab("Time [seconds]") -> p

# summary plot
  df |>
    filter(Time.Sum != 0) |>
    group_by(Slice, StartTS, EndTS, DurationTS, Value) |>
    summarize(N=n(), Time.Sum = sum(Time.Sum), .groups="drop_last") |>
    ungroup(Value) |>
    arrange(Value) |>
    mutate(TaskHeight = Time.Sum / (DurationTS * N)) |>
    mutate(TaskPosition = cumsum(TaskHeight) - TaskHeight) |>
    ggplot() +
    coord_cartesian(ylim=c(0,1)) +
    geom_rect(alpha=.5, aes(
      fill = Value,
      xmin = StartTS,
      xmax = EndTS,
      ymin = TaskPosition,
      ymax = (TaskPosition + TaskHeight)
    )) +
    my_style() +
    theme(legend.position="none") +
    ylab("Load [%]") +
    xlab("Time [seconds]") -> p.summary
 
  if (has.summary == "Both") {
    p / p.summary + plot_layout(heights = c(1, 0.15))
  }else if (has.summary == "Summary") {
    p.summary + theme(legend.justification = "left", legend.position="top")
  }else{
    p +  theme(
    plot.margin = unit(c(0, 0, 0, 0), "cm"),
    legend.spacing = unit(0.1, "mm"),
    panel.grid = element_blank(),
    legend.position = "top",
    legend.direction = "horizontal",    
    legend.justification = "left",
    legend.title = element_blank(),
    legend.key.size   = unit(0.2, "cm"),
    legend.box.spacing = unit(0, "pt"),
    legend.box.margin = margin(0, 0, 0, 0)
    )
  }
}
#+end_src

#+RESULTS:

******* My style

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
my_style <- function() {
  list(
#    scale_fill_brewer(palette = "Set1"),
#    scale_color_brewer(palette = "Set1"),
    scale_fill_manual(
      values = c(
        MPI_Irecv  = "#4DAF4A",  # Set1 green
        MPI_Isend  = "#E41A1C",  # Set1 red
        MPI_Waitall = "#377EB8", # Set1 blue
        Compute     = "#FFD92F"  # yellow        
      )
    ),
    theme_bw(base_size = 16),
    theme(legend.position="top"),
    theme(
      legend.title = element_blank(),
      plot.margin = unit(c(0, 0, 0, 0), "cm"),
      legend.spacing = unit(1, "mm"),
      legend.justification = "left",
      legend.box.spacing = unit(0, "pt"),
      legend.box.margin = margin(0, 0, 0, 0),
      axis.text.x = element_text(angle=45, vjust=1, hjust=1)
    ))
}
#+end_src

#+RESULTS:
****** Functions
******* Read

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
our_read_function <- function(f) {
  read_csv(f,
           show_col_types=FALSE,
           progress=FALSE) |>
    mutate(Container = as.integer(gsub("rank-?", "", Container))) |>
    mutate(Value = str_trim(gsub("^\\s*PMPI_", "MPI_", str_trim(Value)))) |>    
    mutate(Value = as.factor(Value)) |>
    filter(Value %in% c("MPI_Irecv", "MPI_Isend", "MPI_Waitall")) |>
    mutate(Value = factor(Value, levels=c("MPI_Irecv", "MPI_Isend", "MPI_Waitall"))) -> df
# Keep only the part that interest us
# Highly dependent on parallel design
  core_start <- df |>    
    filter(Value == "MPI_Irecv") |>    
    pull(Start) |>    
    min()    
  core_end <- df |>    
    filter(Value == "MPI_Waitall") |>    
    pull(End) |>    
    max()    
  df <- df |>    
    filter(Start < core_end) |>    
    filter(End > core_start) |>    
    mutate(Start = pmax(Start, core_start), End = pmin(End, core_end), Duration = End - Start) |>
    select(Container, Value, Start, End)
# Return the data frame
  return(df)
}
#+end_src

#+RESULTS:

******* Compute

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
add_compute_state <- function(df) {

  compute <- df |>
    arrange(Container, Start) |>
    group_by(Container) |>
    mutate(next_start = lead(Start)) |>
    filter(!is.na(next_start), next_start > End) |>
    transmute(
      Container,
      Start = End,
      End = next_start,
      Value = factor("Compute", levels = c(levels(df$Value), "Compute"))
    )

  bind_rows(df, compute) |>
    arrange(Container, Start) |>
    ungroup()
}
#+end_src

#+RESULTS:
******* Plot ST

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
our_st_plot <- function(data) {
  library(dplyr)
  library(ggplot2)

  data %>%
    rename(Rank = Container) |>
    mutate(
      ymin = Rank - 0.45,
      ymax = Rank + 0.45
    ) %>%
    ggplot() +
    geom_rect(
      aes(
        xmin = Start,
        xmax = End,
        ymin = ymin,
        ymax = ymax,
        fill = Value
      ),
      colour = NA
    ) +
    labs(
      x = "Time",
      y = "Rank",
      fill = "Value"
    ) +
    theme_bw(base_size = 12) +
    theme(
      panel.grid = element_blank(),
      strip.text = element_text(face = "bold"),
      legend.position = "bottom"
    ) +
    my_style()
}
#+end_src

#+RESULTS:
******* Summary per operation

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
summary_per_operation <- function(dfa) {
  dfa |>
    group_by(Value) |>
    summarise(
      n      = n(),
      mean   = mean(Duration, na.rm = TRUE),
      sd     = sd(Duration, na.rm = TRUE),
      min    = min(Duration, na.rm = TRUE),
      p25    = quantile(Duration, 0.25, na.rm = TRUE),
      median = median(Duration, na.rm = TRUE),
      p75    = quantile(Duration, 0.75, na.rm = TRUE),
      p90    = quantile(Duration, 0.90, na.rm = TRUE),
      p99    = quantile(Duration, 0.99, na.rm = TRUE),
      max    = max(Duration, na.rm = TRUE),
      .groups = "drop"
    )
}
#+end_src

#+RESULTS:
******* Plot the summary per task
#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
plot_summary_per_operation <- function(df) {

  ggplot(df, aes(x = Value)) +

    # min → max range
    geom_linerange(aes(ymin = min, ymax = max),
                   linewidth = 0.6, alpha = 0.5) +

    # interquartile range
    geom_linerange(aes(ymin = p25, ymax = p75),
                   linewidth = 3) +

    # median
    geom_point(aes(y = median), size = 3, shape = 21, fill = "white") +

    # p90 and p99 markers
    geom_point(aes(y = p90), shape = 17, size = 2) +
    geom_point(aes(y = p99), shape = 18, size = 2) +

    # sample size label
    geom_text(aes(y = max, label = paste0("n=", n)),
              vjust = -0.5, size = 3) +

#    scale_y_log10() +

    labs(
      x = "Operation",
      y = "Duration",
    ) +

    theme_bw()
}
#+end_src

#+RESULTS:
******* Plot total time per operation
#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
plot_total_time_per_operation <- function(df) {

  df |>
    group_by(Value) |>
    summarise(total_duration = sum(Duration, na.rm = TRUE),
              .groups = "drop") |>
    ggplot(aes(x = Value, y = total_duration, fill = Value)) +
    
    geom_col(width = 0.7) +
    
    geom_text(aes(label = scales::scientific(total_duration)),
              vjust = -0.3, size = 3) +
    
    labs(
      x = "Operation",
      y = "Total Duration",
    ) +
    
    theme_bw() +
    theme(legend.position = "none")
}
#+end_src

#+begin_src R :results output :session *R* :exports both :noweb yes :colnames yes
options(crayon.enabled=FALSE)
suppressMessages(library(tidyverse))
suppressMessages(library(fs))

df.doe <- read_csv("swr-tupi/run-784327/distributed-cube-average/tupi-doe/tupi-doe.csv", progress=FALSE, show_col_types=FALSE)
df.doe |>
  filter(size == 512) |>
  filter(hosts == 16)

tibble(
  FILE=c(
    "swr-tupi/run-784327/distributed-cube-average/tupi-doe/order-103/dc.state.csv",
    "swr-tupi/run-784327/distributed-cube-average/tupi-doe/order-108/dc.state.csv")
) |>
  mutate(Order = str_extract(FILE, "(?<=order-)\\d+") |> as.integer()) |>
  left_join(df.doe, by="Order") |>
  print() |>
  mutate(order = str_extract(FILE, "(?<=order-)\\d+")) |>
  mutate(DATA = map(FILE, our_read_function)) |>
  mutate(DATA = map(DATA, add_compute_state)) |>
  mutate(DATA = map(DATA, function(df) { df |> mutate(Duration = End-Start) })) |>
  mutate(SUMMARY = map(DATA, summary_per_operation)) |>
  mutate(SUMMARY.PLOT = map(SUMMARY, plot_summary_per_operation)) |>
  mutate(SUMMARY.TIME.PLOT = map(DATA, plot_total_time_per_operation)) |>
  mutate(SUMMARY.COMBINED = map2(SUMMARY.PLOT, SUMMARY.TIME.PLOT, `|`)) |>
  mutate(DATA.AGG = map(DATA, do_the_reference_aggregation, 100)) |>
  # tradicional ST view
  mutate(ST = map(DATA, our_st_plot)) |>  
  mutate(ST.AGG = map(DATA.AGG, \(x) do_the_viz(x, has.summary=FALSE))) |>
  pull(ST.AGG) -> plots
library(patchwork)
plots[[1]] + plots[[2]] + theme(plot.margin = unit(c(0, 0, 0, 0), "cm"),panel.spacing = unit(0, "pt")) -> p
ggsave("../papers/2026_CARLA/img/masking-example.png", width = 4, height = 1.6, units = "in", dpi = 300)
#+end_src
